    SELECT [e].[Id], [e].[Apagado], [e].[AtualizadoEm], [e].[CriadoEm], [e].[Nome]
    FROM [Especialidades] AS [e]

) AS [t] ON [m].[EspecialidadeId] = [t].[Id]

    SELECT [d].[Id], [d].[Apagado], [d].[AtualizadoEm], [d].[CriadoEm], [d].[MedicoId], [d].[DiaSemana], [d].[HoraFim], [d].[HoraInicio]

    WHERE [d].[Apagado] = CAST(0 AS bit)
) AS [t0] ON [m].[Id] = [t0].[MedicoId]

) AS [t] ON [c].[MedicoId] = [t].[Id]

SELECT [m].[Id], [m].[Apagado], [m].[AtualizadoEm], [m].[CriadoEm], [m].[Crm], [m].[EspecialidadeId], [m].[Nome], [m].[ValorConsulta], [t].[Id], [t0].[Id], [t0].[Apagado], [t0].[AtualizadoEm], [t0].[CriadoEm], [t0].[MedicoId], [t0].[DiaSemana], [t0].[HoraFim], [t0].[HoraInicio], [m].[Email], [t].[Apagado], [t].[AtualizadoEm], [t].[CriadoEm], [t].[Nome]
FROM [Medicos] AS [m]
INNER JOIN (
    SELECT [e].[Id], [e].[Apagado], [e].[AtualizadoEm], [e].[CriadoEm], [e].[Nome]
    FROM [Especialidades] AS [e]
    WHERE [e].[Apagado] = CAST(0 AS bit)
) AS [t] ON [m].[EspecialidadeId] = [t].[Id]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [d].[Id], [d].[Apagado], [d].[AtualizadoEm], [d].[CriadoEm], [d].[MedicoId], [d].[DiaSemana], [d].[HoraFim], [d].[HoraInicio]
    FROM [DisponibilidadeMedico] AS [d]
    WHERE [d].[Apagado] = CAST(0 AS bit)
) AS [t0] ON [m].[Id] = [t0].[MedicoId]
